### EventingKnativeDevV1alpha1EventPolicySpec

Spec defines the desired state of the EventPolicy.

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**filters**|[[EventingKnativeDevV1alpha1EventPolicySpecFiltersItems0](#eventingknativedevv1alpha1eventpolicyspecfiltersitems0)]|Filters is an array of SubscriptionsAPIFilters that evaluate to true or false. If any filter expression in the array evaluates to false, the event will not continue pass the ingress of the target resources of the policy||
|**from**|[[EventingKnativeDevV1alpha1EventPolicySpecFromItems0](#eventingknativedevv1alpha1eventpolicyspecfromitems0)]|From is the list of sources or oidc identities, which are allowed to send events to the targets (.spec.to).||
|**to**|[[EventingKnativeDevV1alpha1EventPolicySpecToItems0](#eventingknativedevv1alpha1eventpolicyspectoitems0)]|To lists all resources for which this policy applies. Resources in this list must act like an ingress and have an audience. The resources are part of the same namespace as the EventPolicy. An empty list means it applies to all resources in the EventPolicies namespace||
### EventingKnativeDevV1alpha1EventPolicySpecFiltersItems0

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**all**|[]|||
|**any**|[]|Any evaluates to true if any of the nested expressions evaluate to true. It must contain at least one filter expression||
|**cesql**|str|CESQL is a CloudEvents SQL v1 expression that will evaluate to true or false for each CloudEvent.||
|**exact**|any|Exact evaluates to true if the values of the matching CloudEvents attributes all exactly match with the associated value string specified (case sensitive)||
|**not**|any|||
|**prefix**|any|Prefix evaluates to true if the values of the matching CloudEvents attributes all start with the associated value string specified (case sensitive)||
|**suffix**|any|Exact evaluates to true if the values of the matching CloudEvents attributes all end with the associated value string specified (case sensitive)||

### EventingKnativeDevV1alpha1RequestReplySpecDelivery

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**backoffDelay**|str|BackoffDelay is the delay before retrying. More information on Duration format: - https://www.iso.org/iso-8601-date-and-time-format.html - https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_8601  For linear policy, backoff delay is backoffDelay*<numberOfRetries>. For exponential policy, backoff delay is backoffDelay*2^<numberOfRetries>.||
|**backoffPolicy**|str|BackoffPolicy is the retry backoff policy (linear, exponential).||
|**deadLetterSink**|[EventingKnativeDevV1alpha1RequestReplySpecDeliveryDeadLetterSink](#eventingknativedevv1alpha1requestreplyspecdeliverydeadlettersink)|dead letter sink||
|**retry**|int|Retry is the minimum number of retries the sender should attempt when sending an event before moving it to the dead letter sink.||

|**httpOption**|str|HTTPOption is the option of HTTP. It has the following two values:<br />`HTTPOptionEnabled`, `HTTPOptionRedirected`||
|**rules**|[[NetworkingInternalKnativeDevV1alpha1IngressSpecRulesItems0](#networkinginternalknativedevv1alpha1ingressspecrulesitems0)]|A list of host rules used to configure the Ingress.||
|**tls**|[[NetworkingInternalKnativeDevV1alpha1IngressSpecTLSItems0](#networkinginternalknativedevv1alpha1ingressspectlsitems0)]|TLS configuration. Currently Ingress only supports a single TLS<br />port: 443. If multiple members of this list specify different hosts, they<br />will be multiplexed on the same port according to the hostname specified<br />through the SNI TLS extension, if the ingress controller fulfilling the<br />ingress supports SNI.||
### NetworkingInternalKnativeDevV1alpha1IngressSpecRulesItems0

IngressRule represents the rules mapping the paths under a specified host to the related backend services. Incoming requests are first evaluated for a host match, then routed to the backend associated with the matching IngressRuleValue.

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**hosts**|[str]|Host is the fully qualified domain name of a network host, as defined<br />by RFC 3986. Note the following deviations from the "host" part of the<br />URI as defined in the RFC:<br />1. IPs are not allowed. Currently a rule value can only apply to the<br />IP in the Spec of the parent .<br />2. The `:` delimiter is not respected because ports are not allowed.<br />Currently the port of an Ingress is implicitly :80 for http and<br />:443 for https.<br />Both these may change in the future.<br />If the host is unspecified, the Ingress routes all traffic based on the<br />specified IngressRuleValue.<br />If multiple matching Hosts were provided, the first rule will take precedent.||
|**http**|[NetworkingInternalKnativeDevV1alpha1IngressSpecRulesItems0HTTP](#networkinginternalknativedevv1alpha1ingressspecrulesitems0http)|http||
|**visibility**|str|Visibility signifies whether this rule should `ClusterLocal`. If it's not<br />specified then it defaults to `ExternalIP`.||
### NetworkingInternalKnativeDevV1alpha1IngressSpecRulesItems0HTTP

HTTP represents a rule to apply against incoming requests. If the rule is satisfied, the request is routed to the specified backend.

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**paths** `required`|[[NetworkingInternalKnativeDevV1alpha1IngressSpecRulesItems0HTTPPathsItems0](#networkinginternalknativedevv1alpha1ingressspecrulesitems0httppathsitems0)]|A collection of paths that map requests to backends.<br /><br />If they are multiple matching paths, the first match takes precedence.||
### NetworkingInternalKnativeDevV1alpha1IngressSpecRulesItems0HTTPPathsItems0

HTTPIngressPath associates a path regex with a backend. Incoming URLs matching the path are forwarded to the backend.

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**appendHeaders**|{str:str}|AppendHeaders allow specifying additional HTTP headers to add<br />before forwarding a request to the destination service.<br /><br />NOTE: This differs from K8s Ingress which doesn't allow header appending.||
|**headers**|{str:[NetworkingInternalKnativeDevV1alpha1IngressSpecRulesItems0HTTPPathsItems0HeadersAnon](#networkinginternalknativedevv1alpha1ingressspecrulesitems0httppathsitems0headersanon)}|Headers defines header matching rules which is a map from a header name<br />to HeaderMatch which specify a matching condition.<br />When a request matched with all the header matching rules,<br />the request is routed by the corresponding ingress rule.<br />If it is empty, the headers are not used for matching||
|**path**|str|Path represents a literal prefix to which this rule should apply.<br />Currently it can contain characters disallowed from the conventional<br />"path" part of a URL as defined by RFC 3986. Paths must begin with<br />a '/'. If unspecified, the path defaults to a catch all sending<br />traffic to the backend.||
|**rewriteHost**|str|RewriteHost rewrites the incoming request's host header.<br /><br />This field is currently experimental and not supported by all Ingress<br />implementations.||
|**splits** `required`|[[NetworkingInternalKnativeDevV1alpha1IngressSpecRulesItems0HTTPPathsItems0SplitsItems0](#networkinginternalknativedevv1alpha1ingressspecrulesitems0httppathsitems0splitsitems0)]|Splits defines the referenced service endpoints to which the traffic<br />will be forwarded to.||
### NetworkingInternalKnativeDevV1alpha1IngressSpecRulesItems0HTTPPathsItems0HeadersAnon

### NetworkingInternalKnativeDevV1alpha1IngressSpecRulesItems0HTTPPathsItems0SplitsItems0

IngressBackendSplit describes all endpoints for a given service and port.

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**appendHeaders**|{str:str}|AppendHeaders allow specifying additional HTTP headers to add<br />before forwarding a request to the destination service.<br /><br />NOTE: This differs from K8s Ingress which doesn't allow header appending.||
|**percent**|int|Specifies the split percentage, a number between 0 and 100.  If<br />only one split is specified, we default to 100.<br /><br />NOTE: This differs from K8s Ingress to allow percentage split.||
|**serviceName** `required`|str|Specifies the name of the referenced service.||

|**waitTimeSeconds**|int|Wait Time Seconds        The duration (in seconds) for which the call waits for a message to arrive in the queue before returning. If a message is available, the call returns sooner than WaitTimeSeconds. If no messages are available and the wait time expires, the call does not return a message list.||

|**loggerName**|str|Logger Name        Name of the logging category to use|"log-sink"|
|**marker**|str|Marker        An optional Marker name to use||
|**multiline**|bool|Multiline        If enabled then each information is outputted on a newline|False|
|**showAllProperties**|bool|Show All Properties        Show all of the exchange properties (both internal and custom)|False|
|**showBody**|bool|Show Body        Show the message body|True|
|**showBodyType**|bool|Show Body Type        Show the body Java type|True|
|**showCachedStreams**|bool|Show Cached Streams        Whether Camel should show cached stream bodies or not.|True|
|**showExchangePattern**|bool|Show Exchange Pattern        Shows the Message Exchange Pattern (or MEP for short)|True|
|**showHeaders**|bool|Show Headers        Show the headers received|False|
|**showProperties**|bool|Show Properties        Show the exchange properties (only custom). Use showAllProperties to show both internal and custom properties.|False|
|**showStreams**|bool|Show Streams        Show the stream bodies (they may not be available in following steps)|False|

### ServingKnativeDevV1beta1DomainMappingSpec

|**tls**|[ServingKnativeDevV1beta1DomainMappingSpecTLS](#servingknativedevv1beta1domainmappingspectls)|tls||
### ServingKnativeDevV1beta1DomainMappingSpecRef

Ref specifies the target of the Domain Mapping.  The object identified by the Ref must be an Addressable with a URL of the form `{name}.{namespace}.{domain}` where `{domain}` is the cluster domain, and `{name}` and `{namespace}` are the name and namespace of a Kubernetes Service.  This contract is satisfied by Knative types such as Knative Services and Knative Routes, and by Kubernetes Services.

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**address**|str|Address points to a specific Address Name.||
|**apiVersion**|str|API version of the referent.||
|**group**|str|Group of the API, without the version of the group. This can be used as an alternative to the APIVersion, and then resolved using ResolveGroup.<br />Note: This API is EXPERIMENTAL and might break anytime. For more details: https://github.com/knative/eventing/issues/5086||
|**kind** `required`|str|Kind of the referent.<br />More info: https://git.k8s.io/community/contributors/devel/sig-architecture/api-conventions.md#types-kinds||
|**name** `required`|str|Name of the referent.<br />More info: https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/overview/working-with-objects/names/#names||
|**namespace**|str|Namespace of the referent.<br />More info: https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/overview/working-with-objects/namespaces/<br />This is optional field, it gets defaulted to the object holding it if left out.||
### ServingKnativeDevV1beta1DomainMappingSpecTLS

TLS allows the DomainMapping to terminate TLS traffic with an existing secret.

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**secretName** `required`|str|SecretName is the name of the existing secret used to terminate TLS traffic.||
